  <script>
   var supportsPassive = false;
  try {
    var opts = Object.defineProperty({}, 'passive', {
    get: function() {
      supportsPassive = {passive:true};
    }
  });
  window.addEventListener("testPassive", null, opts);
  window.removeEventListener("testPassive", null, opts);
  } catch (e) {}

  window.requestIdleCallback   = window.requestIdleCallback || function (cb) {setTimeout(cb,10);};
  window.requestAnimationFrame = window.requestAnimationFrame || window.webkitRequestAnimationFrame || window.mozRequestAnimationFrame || window.msRequestAnimationFrame || window.oRequestAnimationFrame || function (cb) {setTimeout(cb,1);};

  window.rTasks = [];
  function runTask(callback, loPrior)
  {
  if (window.rTasks[callback.name] !== void 0) return;// already scheduled before
  window.rTasks[callback.name] = 1;

  var toRun = function()
  {
    var start = new Date().getTime();
    callback();
  
    var diff = new Date().getTime() - start;
    console.log(callback.name + " end, took " + diff + "ms");
  };

  if (loPrior == void 0)
    window.requestAnimationFrame(toRun);
  else if (loPrior === 666)
    toRun();
  else
    window.requestIdleCallback(toRun);
  }
  
  window.jqTasks = [];
  function runTaskJquery(callback, loPrior)
  {    
    if (callback != void 0) window.jqTasks.push(function(){runTask(callback, loPrior);});  
    if (window.jQuery == void 0)
      return setTimeout(runTaskJquery, 25); //try again in a while    
    while (window.jqTasks.length) 
      window.jqTasks.shift()();
  }

  window.jqTasksLL = [];
  function runTaskJqueryLL(callback, loPrior)
  {    
    if (callback != void 0) window.jqTasksLL.push(function(){runTask(callback, loPrior);});  
    var notReady = 0 + ((window.jQuery == void 0) || (jQuery.fn == void 0) || (jQuery.fn.lazyload == void 0));
    if (notReady)
      return setTimeout(runTaskJqueryLL, 25); //try again in a while    
    while (window.jqTasksLL.length) 
      window.jqTasksLL.shift()();
  }
  </script>

  <script type="text/javascript">
   var _mlCallInitCallback = function(){};

window.handleCallbackOSM = function(callback) {callback();};

(function(){
  window.duringLoadOSM = false;
  var delayed = [];
  var loadQueue = [];
  
  var handleDelayed = function() {for (var c = 0; c < delayed.length; c++) handleCallbackOSM(delayed[c]);};
  
  var load = function(args){ // Modernizr.load wrapper
  if (typeof window.yepnope !== "undefined")
  {
    if (loadQueue.length > 0)
    {
      var q = loadQueue;
      loadQueue = [];
      yepnope(q);
    }
    yepnope(args);
  }
  else
    loadQueue.push(args);
  };

  window.loadMapJS = function (callback) {
  if (callback === null && loadQueue.length == 0) return;
  if (typeof L != 'undefined') return handleCallbackOSM(callback);
  if (callback !== null && window.duringLoadOSM) {delayed.push(callback); return;}
  window.duringLoadOSM = true;
  load({load: [window.LEAFLET_URL, window.LEAFLET_URL.replace("leaflet", "maplib")],complete: function()
     {
       window.waitMapsID = setInterval(function()
       {
         if (typeof L == 'undefined') return console.log('Leaflet not loaded yet...');
         if (typeof mL_createMap == 'undefined') return console.log('Maplib not loaded yet...');

         clearInterval(window.waitMapsID);

         window.mL_LoadMapJS = loadMapJS;
         if (callback !== null) handleCallbackOSM(callback);
         handleDelayed();
        },25);
     }});
  };

  window.skipAutoloadOSM = true;
  window.mL_LoadMapJS = loadMapJS;
})();

function GradientBarMouseMove() {}
function GradientBarMouseOut() {}
function GradientBarMouseLeave() {}

function loadBoxMap()
{
  var U=window.LEAFLET_URL.replace("//pics", "https://pics"), QUEUE = [U, U.replace('leaflet', 'maplib'), U.replace('leaflet.js', 'boxMap.js')];

  if (typeof L  !== 'undefined' || window.duringLoadOSM === true) QUEUE.shift(); //LEAFLET already loaded/loading
  if (window.duringLoadOSM === true) QUEUE.shift(); //MAPLIB already loaded/loading
  yepnope({load: QUEUE, complete: function(){window.mL_LoadMapJS = window.loadMapJS;initBoxMapPopupOptions();handleCallbackOSM(window.loadGMAP);}});
}

  <script>
   // preload slider images
 function preload(arrayOfImages) 
 {
  for(index = 0; index < arrayOfImages.length; ++index)
  {
    var img = new Image();
    img.src = arrayOfImages[index];
  }
 }
gImageIndex=0;
gImagerArr=false;


function preload_withDelay()
{
    if(gImageIndex < gImagerArr.length)
    {
      var img = new Image();
      img.src = gImagerArr[gImageIndex];
      gImageIndex++;
      window.setTimeout(preload_withDelay,9000);
    }
}


 function preload_with_delay(arrayOfImages) {
  gImagerArr=arrayOfImages;
  window.setTimeout(preload_withDelay,9000);
 }
 // Usage:
//preload(["\/\/pics3.city-data.com\/\/\/pics3.city-data.com\/assets\/desktop\/bg\/1background.jpg"]);
preload_with_delay(["\/\/pics3.city-data.com\/assets\/desktop\/bg\/2background.jpg","\/\/pics3.city-data.com\/assets\/desktop\/bg\/3background.jpg","\/\/pics3.city-data.com\/assets\/desktop\/bg\/4background.jpg","\/\/pics3.city-data.com\/assets\/desktop\/bg\/5background.jpg","\/\/pics3.city-data.com\/assets\/desktop\/bg\/6background.jpg","\/\/pics3.city-data.com\/assets\/desktop\/bg\/7background.jpg","\/\/pics3.city-data.com\/assets\/desktop\/bg\/8background.jpg","\/\/pics3.city-data.com\/assets\/desktop\/bg\/9background.jpg"]);
  </script>

    </h2>
    <p class="textowo">
     By collecting and analyzing data from a variety of government and private sources, we're able to create detailed, informative profiles for every city in the United States. From crime rates to weather patterns, youll find the data you're looking for on City-Data.com.
    </p>
    <p class="textowo">
     City-Data sees over 14 million users per month and has been featured in 121 books, on CNN, WABC in New York, Bay News 9 in Tampa Bay and USA Today's Hot Sites, among others.
    </p>
   </div>
  </div>

      window.BOXMAP_WEBGL = 1;
window.LEAFLET_URL = '//pics3.city-data.com/js/maps/CANVAS/leaflet.js?v=9.4.4';
window.supportsPassive = false;

try { document.domain = 'city-data.com'; } catch (e) {}
try {var opts = Object.defineProperty({}, 'passive', {get: function() {supportsPassive = {passive:true};}});window.addEventListener("testPassive", null, opts);window.removeEventListener("testPassive", null, opts);} catch (e) {};

     <script>
      function loadBoxMapWhenComplete()     
{
    window.waitMapsBmID = setInterval(function()
    {
        //if (typeof jQuery === 'undefined') return console.log('jQuery not loaded yet[bm]...');
        if (typeof L === 'undefined') return console.log('Leaflet not loaded yet[bm]...');
        if (typeof mL_createMap === 'undefined') return console.log('Maplib not loaded yet[bm]...');
        if (typeof loadGMAP === 'undefined') return console.log('boxMAP not loaded yet[bm]...');
        clearInterval(window.waitMapsBmID);

        window.mL_LoadMapJS = window.loadMapJS;
        initBoxMapPopupOptions();
        handleCallbackOSM(window.loadGMAP);
	}, 25);    
}
    
function loadBoxMap() 
{
  var U=window.LEAFLET_URL.replace("//pics", "https://pics"), QUEUE = [U, U.replace('leaflet', 'maplib'), U.replace('leaflet.js', 'boxMap.js')];
  
  if (typeof L  !== 'undefined' || window.duringLoadOSM === true) QUEUE.shift(); //LEAFLET already loaded/loading
  if (window.duringLoadOSM === true) QUEUE.shift(); //MAPLIB already loaded/loading
    
  loadBoxMapWhenComplete();
  
  while(QUEUE.length)
  {
    var s = document.createElement('script'); 
    s.type = 'text/javascript'; 
    s.async = true;
    s.src = QUEUE.shift();
    (document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0] || document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0]).appendChild(s);
  }
  
  window.loadBoxMap = function(){ console.log("already executed"); };
}

function initBoxMapPopupOptions()
{  
    
  if (typeof jQuery === 'undefined')    
    return setTimeout(initBoxMapPopupOptions, 50);

  if (typeof bAPI === 'undefined')
    window.bAPI = window; // for compatiblity with previous version

  if (1 && typeof window.SKIP_OSM_EVENT_SHIELD === 'undefined' && typeof eventShield !== 'undefined') 
{
  new eventShield('eventSHIELD', 'boxMAPborder', 1000);
  if (typeof document.getElementsByClassName !== 'undefined')
  {
    var md = document.getElementsByClassName('mapdiv');
    if (md.length === 1)
    {
      md = md[0];
      md.id = "mapdiv1234";
      md.style.position = 'relative';
      new eventShield('eventSHIELD2', md.id, 1000);
    }
  }
}
}

    
    if (typeof DrawColorPattern === 'function') initBoxMapPopupOptions();
     </script>

  <div class="container space">
   <div class="col-md-7">
    <h2 class="featurette-heading">
     What's on
     <span class="text-muted">
      City-Data.com
     </span>
    </h2>
    <p>
     We have over 74,000 city photos not found anywhere else, graphs of the latest real estate prices and sales trends, recent home sales, a home value estimator, hundreds of thousands of maps, satellite photos, demographic data (race, income, ancestries, education, employment), geographic data, state profiles, crime data, registered sex offenders, cost of living, housing, religions, businesses, local news links based on our exclusive technology, birthplaces of famous people, political contributions, city government finances, employment, weather, natural disasters, hospitals, schools and libraries.
    </p>
    <p>
     In addition to our huge collection of data, we have also created our
     <a href="//www.city-data.com/toplists.html">
      Top 100 City Lists
     </a>
     and
     <a href="//www.city-data.com/top2/toplists2.html">
      Top 101 City Lists
     </a>
     . These lists rank cities in hundreds of categories, including income, crime, most gay couples, most cars, shortest commute, biggest houses, best educated residents and many more. We also have thousands of
     <a href="//www.city-data.com/randomPics.php">
      random city pictures
     </a>
     submitted by our users.
    </p>

   var waitForFinalEvent=(function(){var timers={};return function(callback,ms,uniqueId){if(!uniqueId){uniqueId="Don't call this twice without a uniqueId";}

function initLaterMenu()
{
  window.menuRedesign = function()
  {
  var menu_more=$('#menu_dropdown');
  var menu_visible=$('#menu_visible');
  var menu_more_li=$('#menu_dropdown_li');
  var menu_container=$(".navbar-fixed-top > .container-menu");
  if($(".navbar-toggle").is(":visible")){menu_more.children().insertBefore(menu_more_li);menu_more_li.hide();}
  else{menu_more_li.show();var available_space=menu_container.width()-$(".navbar-header").outerWidth(true)-$("#search_bar_menu").outerWidth(true)-menu_more_li.outerWidth(true);var children=menu_visible.children();var curr_width=0;var reached_end=false;var i=0;var margin=8;for(;i<children.length;++i)
  {var ch=$(children[i]);if(ch.prop("id")==menu_more_li.prop("id"))
  {reached_end=true;break;}
  if(ch.is(':visible'))
  curr_width+=ch.outerWidth(true);if(curr_width+margin>available_space)
  {break;}}
  if(reached_end)
  {var children=menu_more.children();for(i=0;i<children.length;++i)
  {var ch=$(children[i]);ch.insertBefore(menu_more_li);if(ch.is(':visible'))
  curr_width+=ch.outerWidth(true);if(curr_width+margin>available_space)
  {ch.prependTo(menu_more);break;}}}else
  {var topushfront=[];for(;i<children.length;++i)
  {var ch=$(children[i]);if(ch.prop("id")==menu_more_li.prop("id"))
  {break;}
  topushfront.push(ch);}
  for(i=0;i<topushfront.length;++i)
  {var ch=$(topushfront[topushfront.length-1-i]);ch.prependTo(menu_more);}}}
  
  menu_visible.removeClass("changing");menu_container.removeClass("changing");$(".navbar-collapse").removeClass("changing");
  }

  menuRedesign();
}

function initLaterMenuEvents()
{
  $(window).resize(function()
  {
    var menu_visible=$('#menu_visible');
    var menu_container=$(".navbar-fixed-top > .container-menu");
    menu_container.addClass("changing");
    menu_visible.addClass("changing");
    $(".navbar-collapse").addClass("changing");
    waitForFinalEvent(menuRedesign,100,'menu_auto_hide');
  });

  if('ontouchstart'in document) return this;

  
  var $allDropdowns=$();
  $.fn.dropdownHover=function(options)
  {
    $allDropdowns=$allDropdowns.add(this.parent());
    return this.each(function(){var $this=$(this),$parent=$this.parent(),defaults={delay:100,delay2:900,instantlyCloseOthers:false},data={delay:$(this).data('delay'),instantlyCloseOthers:$(this).data('close-others')},showEvent='show.bs.dropdown',hideEvent='hide.bs.dropdown',settings=$.extend(true,{},defaults,options,data),timeout,timeout2;$parent.hover(function(event){if(settings.instantlyCloseOthers===true)
  $allDropdowns.removeClass('open');window.clearTimeout(timeout2);window.clearTimeout(timeout);$parent.addClass('openning');$parent.removeClass('closing');timeout=window.setTimeout(function(){window.clearTimeout(timeout2);window.clearTimeout(timeout);$parent.addClass('open');$parent.removeClass('openning');},5);},function(){window.clearTimeout(timeout2);window.clearTimeout(timeout);timeout=window.setTimeout(function(){window.clearTimeout(timeout2);window.clearTimeout(timeout);$parent.removeClass('open');$parent.removeClass('opening');$parent.addClass('closing');timeout2=window.setTimeout(function(){$parent.removeClass('closing');$parent.removeClass('opening');window.clearTimeout(timeout2);window.clearTimeout(timeout);},settings.delay2);},settings.delay);});$parent.find('.dropdown-submenu').each(function(){var $this=$(this);var subTimeout;$this.hover(function(){window.clearTimeout(subTimeout);$this.children('.dropdown-menu').show();$this.siblings().children('.dropdown-menu').hide();},function(){var $submenu=$this.children('.dropdown-menu');subTimeout=window.setTimeout(function(){$submenu.hide();},settings.delay);});});});
  };
  
  $('[data-hover="dropdown"]').dropdownHover();
}

runTask(initLaterMenu, 1);
runTask(initLaterMenuEvents, 1);
  </script>
  <script>
   function handleScroll()
{  
  var sTop = window.pageYOffset || document.documentElement.scrollTop;
  if (window.lastScrollTop === sTop) return;
        
  if (sTop > 100)
  {    
    if (window.lastScrollTop === void 0 || window.lastScrollTop < 100)
      scrollTop.className = 'scroll-top-wrapper show';
  }
  else
    scrollTop.className = 'scroll-top-wrapper';
    
  window.lastScrollTop = sTop;

}
   

function scrollToTop() {
    verticalOffset = typeof(verticalOffset) != 'undefined' ? verticalOffset : 0;
    element = $('body');
    offset = element.offset();
    offsetTop = offset.top;
    $('html, body').animate({scrollTop: offsetTop}, 500, 'linear');
}
   
function initLaterScrollTop()
{
  window.scrollTop = document.querySelector('.scroll-top-wrapper');

  runTask(handleScroll,1);
  
  var waiting = false, endScrollHandle = void 0;  
  
  window.addEventListener('scroll', function () {
  if (waiting) return;
  waiting = true;

    // clear previous scheduled endScrollHandle
    clearTimeout(endScrollHandle);

    handleScroll();

    setTimeout(function () {waiting = false;}, 100);

    // schedule an extra execution of scroll() after 200ms in case the scrolling stops in next 100ms
    endScrollHandle = setTimeout(handleScroll, 200);
  }, supportsPassive);

  
  
  scrollTop.addEventListener('click', scrollToTop);

}

runTask(initLaterScrollTop,1);
  </script>

}

/* city autocomplete */
$(function(){
    function run(){
            function formatItemAutocomplete(row) {
                if(typeof(row[1]) != "undefined" && row[1] !== null) {
                    return row[0] + " (<i>pop. " + row[1] + "</i>)";
                }
            }

            $("#city_left").each(function(){
                    $(this).autocomplete('/city-compare/ajax_city.php', {
                                    delay:100,
                                    minChars:3,
                                    formatItem:formatItemAutocomplete
                    }).result(function (evt, data, formatted) {
                    })
            })


            $("#city_right").each(function(){
                    $(this).autocomplete('/city-compare/ajax_city.php', {
                                    delay:100,
                                    minChars:3,
                                    formatItem:formatItemAutocomplete
                    }).result(function (evt, data, formatted) {
                    })
            })
            $(".btn-submit").click(function () {
                $("#city_form").submit();
            });

            $('#city_left').keypress(function (e) {
              if (e.which == 13) {
                $('form#city_form').submit();
                return false;
              }
            });
            $('#city_right').keypress(function (e) {
              if (e.which == 13) {
                $('form#city_form').submit();
                return false;
              }
            });

    }
    run();
});

  <script>
   if (!document.getElementsByClassName) {
  document.getElementsByClassName = function(search) {
    var d = document, elements, pattern, i, results = [];
    if (d.querySelectorAll) { // IE8
      return d.querySelectorAll("." + search);
    }
    if (d.evaluate) { // IE6, IE7
      pattern = ".//*[contains(concat(' ', @class, ' '), ' " + search + " ')]";
      elements = d.evaluate(pattern, d, null, 0, null);
      while ((i = elements.iterateNext())) {
        results.push(i);
      }
    } else {
      elements = d.getElementsByTagName("*");
      pattern = new RegExp("(^|\\s)" + search + "(\\s|$)");
      for (i = 0; i < elements.length; i++) {
        if ( pattern.test(elements[i].className) ) {
          results.push(elements[i]);
        }
      }
    }
    return results;
  }
}

	window.detailView=
	{
		additionalStateData:[],
		tabContentSelected:$("#quickview_tabSelected"),
		visible:false,
		init:function (){},
		show:function (){},
		loadUserLocation:function (){},
		showSelectedDetails:function (state){
			var st=ab2st[state];
			if(!st)return;
			var st_=st.replace(/ /g,"-"); //st.replace(" ","-");
			var schools="";
			if(ab2sch[state])
			schools="  <a href='/schools-dirs/schools-"+state+".html'><span class=\"badge\">"+state+"</span>  K-12 Schools</a>";

			var rests="";
			if(ab2rest[state])
			rests="  <a href='"+ab2restl[state]+"'><span class=\"badge\">"+state+"</span>  Restaurants</a>";


			var asses="";
			if(ab2ass[state])
			asses="  <a href='/properties-index/"+st_+".html'><span class=\"badge\">"+state+"</span>  Assessments</a>";


			if(this.additionalStateData.hasOwnProperty(state))
			{
				var c=this.additionalStateData[state];
				asses+="  <a href='"+c.link+"'><span class=\"badge\">"+state+"</span>  "+c.city+" Profile</a>";
			}
			this.tabContentSelected.html("<h4>Our "+st+" data</h4><p><a href='/city/"+st_+".html'><span class=\"badge\">"+state+"</span>  City Profiles</a> "+schools+rests+asses+"</p>");
		}
	};
	detailView.init();
}

function initLaterdetailViewGeo() 
{
	
	var geoloc_data={"state":"CA"};	if(geoloc_data.hasOwnProperty('state'))
	{
		if(geoloc_data.hasOwnProperty('city'))
		{
			detailView.additionalStateData[geoloc_data.state]=geoloc_data;
		}
	  detailView.showSelectedDetails(geoloc_data.state);
  	}
}  	

function initLaterdetailViewEvents() 
{
  $(".states_map_links").click(function ( event ) 
  {
    $(".states_map_links").removeClass( "hilite" );
    $( event.target ).addClass("hilite");
    detailView.showSelectedDetails( $( event.target ).text());
  });

}

runTask(initLaterdetailViewGeo,1);

  <script type="text/javascript">
   function initLaterDropdownEvents()
    {
        $(document.body).on('click', '#tab_dropdown li', function (event) {

            var $target = $(event.currentTarget);

            $target.closest('.btn-group')
                .find('[data-bind="label"]').text($target.text())
                .end()
                .children('.dropdown-toggle').dropdown('toggle');
            $('.tab-pane').each(function () {
                $(this).removeClass('active');
            });
            //ustaw aktywna klase
            $($target.find('a:first').attr('href')).addClass('active');
            //zmien ustawienia na ukrytych tabach
            $('.tabsol2 li').each(function () {
                if ($(this).find('a:first').text() == $('#dropdown-label').text()) {
                    $(this).addClass('active');
                } else {
                    $(this).removeClass('active');
                }
            });

            return false;

        });

        $(document).on('click.bs.tab.data-api', '[data-toggle="tab"]', function (e) {
            //przekopiowanie ustawienia tabow na selectbox
            $('.tab-pane').each(function () {
                if ($(this).hasClass('active')) {
                    $('#dropdown-label').text($(this).find('h4:first').text());
                }
            });
        })


        $('#myTab a').click(function (e) {
            e.preventDefault()
            $(this).tab('show')
        })

    }
    runTaskJquery(initLaterDropdownEvents, 1);
  </script>
  <script type="text/javascript">
   function stateNamesUpdate()
{
  window.curWidth = $(window).width();
  if (window.prevWidth >= 1200 && window.curWidth < 1200) tabShortNames();
  if (window.prevWidth < 1200 && window.curWidth >= 1200) tabLongNames();
  
  window.prevWidth = window.curWidth;  
}

function initLaterStateNames()
{
    window.tabShortNames = function () {
    $('.tab-list-short').each(function() {
        $(this).show();
    });
    $('.tab-list-long').each(function() {
        $(this).hide();
    });

    $('#map-tab-left').removeClass('col-md-5');
    $('#map-tab-right').removeClass('col-md-7');
    $('#map-tab-left').addClass('col-md-8');
    $('#map-tab-right').addClass('col-md-4');
  };
  
  window.tabLongNames = function () {
    $('.tab-list-short').each(function() {
        $(this).hide();
    });
    $('.tab-list-long').each(function() {
        $(this).show();
    });

    $('#map-tab-left').removeClass('col-md-8');
    $('#map-tab-right').removeClass('col-md-4');
    $('#map-tab-left').addClass('col-md-5');
    $('#map-tab-right').addClass('col-md-7');
  };

  window.prevWidth = 1300;
  stateNamesUpdate();
  $(window).resize(function() {waitForFinalEvent(stateNamesUpdate,200,'1');});
}

runTaskJquery(initLaterStateNames, 1);
  </script>
  <script>
   function initLaterSearchBox() {
	var searchBox=
	{
		delay: 400,
		hideTimeout: false,
		active: false,
		over: false,
		img: null,
		init:function(mob)
		{
      this.img = document.getElementById('search_o_google');

			searchBox.check();
			$('#intelligent_search').mouseenter(function() {
				searchBox.over=true;
				searchBox.check();

			});

			$('#myCarousel').mouseleave(function() {
				searchBox.over=false;
				searchBox.check();
			});

			$('#intelligent_search').focus(function() {
				searchBox.active=true;
				searchBox.check();
			});

			$('#intelligent_search').blur(function() {
					searchBox.active=false;
					searchBox.check();
			});


			$('#intelligent_search').click(function() {
				searchBox.active=true;
				searchBox.check();
			});


		},
		check: function()
		 {
			 if(this.over || this.active)
			 {
			   if (this.img.className !== "loaded")
			   {
			     this.img.className = "loaded";
			     this.img.src = this.img.getAttribute('data-original');
			   }
			 
				 if(this.hideTimeout)
				 {
					 window.clearTimeout(this.hideTimeout);
					 this.hideTimeout=false;
				 }
				// if(!$( "#search_bar_box" ).hasClass("search-active"))
				 window.setTimeout(function () {
				 $( "#search_bar_box" ).addClass("search-active");
				 $( "#search_bar_box" ).removeClass("search-inactive");
			 	},100);
			 }else
			 {
				 if(!this.hideTimeout)
				 {
	 				 this.hideTimeout = window.setTimeout(function () {
						 searchBox.hideTimeout=false;
	 					 $( "#search_bar_box" ).removeClass("search-active");
						 $( "#search_bar_box" ).addClass("search-inactive");
	 				},this.delay);
				}
			 }





		}



	};

	searchBox.init();
	$( "#search_bar_box" ).submit(function( event ) {_gaq.push(['_trackEvent', 'homepage_searchbox', 'clicked','']);});
}
  runTaskJquery(initLaterSearchBox, 1);
  </script>

 function initLateterForum()
 {

 function ra(s,t){if (parseInt(navigator.appVersion) >= 2){document.write("<a rel=\"nofollow\" href=\"",s,"\">",t,"</a>");}}function cdstats(){document.write('<if'+'rame width="1" scrolling="no" height="1" frameborder="0" allowtransparency="true" hspace="0" vspace="0" marginheight="0" marginwidth="0" src="http://'+'www.city-data.com/'+'js/stats/tracker.html" name="cd_stats_frame"></iframe>');}
 function setCookie(c_name,value,days){document.cookie=c_name+ "=" +escape(value)+";path=/;expires=Thu, 01 Jan 2009 14:17:41 GMT";}
 function resizeFrame(f) {f.style.height = f.contentWindow.document.body.scrollHeight + "px";}
 function readCookie(name) {var nameEQ = name + "=";var ca = document.cookie.split(';');for(var i=0;i < ca.length;i++) {var c = ca[i];while (c.charAt(0)==' ') c = c.substring(1,c.length);if (c.indexOf(nameEQ) == 0) return c.substring(nameEQ.length,c.length);}return null;}
 window.fpl_toggle = function(show){
 	// detect iphone
 	var agent=navigator.userAgent.toLowerCase();
 	var is_iphone = (agent.indexOf('iphone')!=-1);
 	c = readCookie('sflv');
 	if (show==1 && c=='hide') show = 0;
 	f = document.getElementById("lfp_container");
 	if (f){
 		if (is_iphone) {
 			f.innerHTML = '';
 			return false;
 		}
 		if (show){
 		
 		//var fi = document.getElementById("lfp_containerIMG");
 		//fi.src = fi.getAttribute('data-src');
 		
 		
    f.innerHTML = '<div id="lfp_ctrls"><span><a href="//www.city-data.com/forum/">See the whole Forum</a> | <a href="#" onclick="fpl_toggle(0);return false;">Hide Forum Preview <img src="//pics3.city-data.com/images/close.png" alt="Hide" /></a></span></div>'
                            + '<iframe name="lfp_frame" id="lfp_frame" src="//www.city-data.com/forum/liveforum.php?b=d" frameborder="0"></iframe>';
 			if (show==2){
 				document.cookie="sflv=show;path=/;expires=Mon, 05 Jan 2032 14:17:41 GMT";
 			}
 		} else {
 			f.innerHTML = '<div id="lfp_showlink"><a href="#" onclick="fpl_toggle(2);return false;">Show Live Forum Preview</a></div>';
 			document.cookie="sflv=hide;path=/;expires=Mon, 05 Jan 2032 14:17:41 GMT";
 		}
 	}
 	return false;
     };
     
  if ($(window).width() > 767) $('#lfp_container').lazyload({ appear: function () { fpl_toggle(1); } });     
}
 

function initLateterOSM()

function initLaterCarousel()
{
  window.initCarousel = function(car) {
      $(car).find("img").each(function () { $(this).attr('src', $(this).data('src')); });
  };

  window.carIT = setInterval(function () {
      if ($.fn.carousel == void 0) return; //bootstrap js still not loaded
      clearInterval(window.carIT);
      $.fn.carousel.Constructor.TRANSITION_DURATION = 4000;
      $("#myCarousel").carousel({ interval: 9000 });
  }, 50);
  
  $('#assessmentsCarousel,#restaurantsCarousel,#bottomCarousel').lazyload({ threshold: 200, appear: function () { initCarousel(this); }});
}

 function initLaterFooter()
 {
  window.loadTT = function() {
      var tt = document.createElement('script');
      tt.type = 'text/javascript';
      tt.async = true;
      tt.src = 'https://platform.twitter.com/widgets.js';
      (document.getElementsByTagName('head')[0] || document.getElementsByTagName('body')[0]).appendChild(tt);
  };


  $('#footer').lazyload({appear:loadTT}); 
 }
 
 function initLaterImg()
 { 
  $('img.lazy').lazyload({ threshold: 200 });
 }


runTaskJqueryLL(initLaterImg, 1);
runTaskJqueryLL(initLaterCarousel, 1);
runTaskJqueryLL(initLaterFooter, 1);
if (window.initLateterForum !== void 0) runTask(initLateterForum,1);
if (window.initLateterOSM !== void 0) runTaskJqueryLL(initLateterOSM, 1);
